🏫 मौलाना आज़ाद नेशनल उर्दू यूनिवर्सिटी (MANUU)🏫



🌌आज  रात को लगभग 12 बजे,
लाइब्रेरी के पास एक अत्यंत चिंताजनक घटना घटी।

सफेद कपड़े पहने एक व्यक्ति को छात्राओं के सामने
❌ अनुचित और अशोभनीय हरकत ❌ करते हुए देखा गया।

यह कार्य बेहद निंदनीय है।
छात्राओं के अनुसार यह पहली बार नहीं है —
संभवतः वही व्यक्ति पहले भी कई मौकों पर ऐसा कर चुका है।

उसने अपनी पहचान छिपाया हुआ हैं।
छात्र और एक सुरक्षा गार्ड के मौजूद होने के बावजूद,
वह पकड़े जाने से पहले ही भाग निकला।


🚨 ध्यान दें :

 किसी भी संदिग्ध या अनुचित व्यवहार को नज़रअंदाज़ न करें।

 तुरंत MANUU सुरक्षा टीम को सूचित करें।

 यदि सुरक्षित हो तो सीधे हस्तक्षेप भी करें।

👉 आपका कदम किसी बड़ी हानि को रोक सकता है।


🛑 यह याद रखें :

शैक्षणिक संस्थान में इस प्रकार के आचरण की कोई जगह नहीं है।
इस पर सख्त अनुशासनात्मक और कानूनी कार्रवाई आवश्यक है।

आइए, हम सब मिलकर अपने परिसर को सुरक्षित और सम्मानजनक बनाए रखें।

23/11/25, 11:15 pm - Gulshan: *MACHINE LEARNING* 

*Unit: 1 - Introduction:*
Defining learning systems, 
Goals and applications of machine learning. 
Aspects of developing a learning system: 
		training data, 
		concept representation, 
		function approximation, 
		supervised learning, 
		unsupervised learning, 
		Reinforcement learning, 
		learning algorithms.


*Unit: 2 - Decision Tree Learning:* 
Representing concepts as decision trees. 
Recursive induction of decision trees. 

Picking the best splitting attribute: entropy and information gain. 
Searching for simple trees and computational complexity,
Overfitting, noisy data, and pruning.


*Unit: 3 - Ensemble Learning:*
Bagging, boosting, and Ada-Boost. 
Experimental Evaluation of Learning Algorithms, 
Measuring the accuracy of learned hypotheses.
Comparing learning algorithms: 
		cross-validation, 
		learning curves, and 
		statistical hypothesis testing.


*Unit: 4 -*
*Rule Learning:*
Translating decision trees into rules. 
Artificial Neural Networks:
	Neurons and biological motivation. 
Linear threshold units.

*Perceptrons:*
representational limitation and gradient descent training.
Multilayer networks and back propagation. 
Hidden layers and constructing intermediate. 
Overfitting, 
learning network structure, 
recurrent networks.


*Unit: 5 -* 

*Support Vector Machines:* 
Maximum margin linear separators. 
Kernels for learning non-linear functions.

*Bayesian Learning:* 
theory and Bayes rule. 
Naive Bayes learning algorithm.
Parameter smoothing. 
Generative vs. discriminative training. 
Logisitic regression. 
Bayes nets and Markov nets for representing dependencies.

*Instance-Based Learning:* 
Constructing explicit generalizations versus comparing to past specific examples. 
k-Nearest neighbour algorithm, 
Case-based learning.

16/02/26, 8:27 pm - Gulshan: Q1. 5 marks
Explain perceptron with its parts. Write two applications. Also write one limitation of perceptron.

Q2. 5 marks
Explain the structure of a neural network. What is the role of activation function. Write two differences between neural network and perceptron.

Q3. 5 marks
Given x1 = 1, x2 = 2, w1 = 0.5, w2 = -1, b = 1.
Find z = w1x1 + w2x2 + b.
Find output using these activation functions. Sigmoid, Tanh, ReLU, Step.

Q4. 5 marks
A diabetes dataset has 5 inputs and 3 hidden layers.
Which activation function will you use in hidden layers and output layer.
Write two applications of neural network.

17/02/26, 2:27 pm - mehzbeen: ✅ 1. Define the Following (5 Marks)
a. Probability

Probability is a numerical measure of the likelihood that an event will occur. Its value ranges between 0 and 1, where 0 indicates impossibility and 1 indicates certainty.

b. Random Variable

A random variable is a numerical quantity whose value depends on the outcome of a random experiment.

Example: The number obtained when a die is rolled.

c. Conditional Probability Rule

Conditional probability is the probability of an event occurring given that another event has already occurred.

𝑃
(
𝐴
∣
𝐵
)
=
𝑃
(
𝐴

𝐵
)
𝑃

)
P(A∣B)=
P(B)
P(A∩B)
	​

d. Mental Model

A mental model is a conceptual framework or way of thinking that helps individuals understand situations and make decisions based on assumptions, experience, or logical reasoning.

e. Management Science

Management science is the application of mathematical models, statistics, and analytical methods to improve decision-making and solve business or organizational problems.

✅ 2. Describe the Spreadsheet Modeling Process (5 Marks)

Spreadsheet modeling is the use of software such as Microsoft Excel to build models that analyze data and support decision-making.

Steps in Spreadsheet Modeling Process:

Define the Problem – Identify objectives and decision variables.

Enter Input Data – Insert required data into spreadsheet cells.

Develop the Model Structure – Create formulas and relationships among variables.

Perform Analysis – Calculate outputs using formulas and functions.

Validate the Model – Check whether results are accurate and logical.

Make Decisions – Interpret results and choose the best alternative.

Advantages: easy calculations, quick analysis, and visual presentation.

✅ 3. Attempt the Following
a. Explain Mathematical Modeling (2M)

Mathematical modeling is the process of representing real-world problems using mathematical equations, formulas, or relationships in order to analyze situations and make predictions.

Example: Profit = Revenue − Cost.

b. Probability of not getting cold (1M)

Given:

𝑃
(
Getting cold
)
=
0.71
P(Getting cold)=0.71
𝑃
(
Not getting cold
)
=
1
−
0.71
=
0.29
P(Not getting cold)=1−0.71=0.29

Answer: The probability of not getting cold is 0.29.

c. One approach for assessing likelihood of an outcome (2M)

Classical Approach to Probability:
Probability is calculated as:

Probability
=
Number of favorable outcomes
Total number of possible outcomes
Probability=
Total number of possible outcomes
Number of favorable outcomes
	​


This approach is used when all outcomes are equally likely, such as tossing a fair coin or rolling a die.

✅ 4. Calculate the Following
a. Probability of 0 or 1 defective items (2M)

Given:

P(0 defective) = 0.50
P(1 defective) = 0.20

𝑃
(
0
 or 
1
)
=
𝑃
(
0
)
+
𝑃
(
1
)
P(0 or 1)=P(0)+P(1)
=
0.50
+
0.20
=
0.70
=0.50+0.20=0.70

Answer: The probability of producing 0 or 1 defective items is 0.70.

b. Complement of Event A (3M)

Event A = Observing at least one tail when two coins are tossed.

Sample space:
HH, HT, TH, TT

Event A = HT, TH, TT
Complement of A (Aᶜ) = Event where no tail occurs.

Therefore, complement of A is:

👉 HH (both coins show heads).
